decisions = {
	borrow_money_d_holyadoptionist = {
		potential = {
			religion = adoptionist
			
			is_title_active = d_holyadoptionist
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = borrowed_from_d_holyadoptionist }
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_holyadoptionist }

			has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"

			d_holyadoptionist = {
				holder_scope = {
					liege = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		allow = {
			d_holyadoptionist = {
				holder_scope = {
					wealth = 300
					ROOT = {
						NOT = { excommunicated_for = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		effect = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = borrowed_from_d_holyadoptionist
				duration = -1
				inherit = yes
			}

			hidden_tooltip = {
				d_holyadoptionist = {
					holder_scope = {
						character_event = {
							id = SoA.1010
						}
					}
				}
			}

			wealth = 300
		}

		revoke_allowed = {
			always = no
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				wealth = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01 # Slow it down
			}
		}
	}

	donate_money_to_d_holyadoptionist = {
		potential = {
			religion = adoptionist
			
			is_title_active = d_holyadoptionist
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = expelled_d_holyadoptionist }
			is_title_active = d_holyadoptionist 



			has_dlc = "Sons of Abraham"

			d_holyadoptionist = {
				holder_scope = {
					liege = {
						NOT = { character = ROOT }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		allow = {
			wealth = 300
		}

		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_character_modifier = donated_to_holy_order }
				}
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = donated_to_holy_order
					duration = -1
				}
			}

			hidden_tooltip = {
				d_holyadoptionist = {
					holder_scope = {
						character_event = {
							id = SoA.1140
						}
					}
				}
			}

			wealth = -300
			piety = 300
		}

		revoke_allowed = {
			always = no
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					piety = 1000
					NOT = { wealth = 1000 }
					AND = {
						NOT = { controls_religion = adoptionist }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.002 # Slow it down
			}
		}
	}

		}

			wealth = 300
		}

				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_character_modifier = donated_to_holy_order }
				}
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = donated_to_holy_order
					duration = -1
				}
			}

			hidden_tooltip = {
				d_holysemipelagian = {
					holder_scope = {
						character_event = {

						}
					}
				}
			}

			piety = 300
		}

			always = no
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					piety = 1000
					NOT = { wealth = 1000 }
					AND = {
						NOT = { controls_religion = semipelagian }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.002 # Slow it down
			}

				limit = { 
					NOT = { has_character_modifier = donated_to_holy_order }
				}
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = donated_to_holy_order
					duration = -1
				}
			}

			hidden_tooltip = {
				d_holysol_boreas_reformed = {
					holder_scope = {
						character_event = {
							id = SoA.1140
						}
					}
				}
			}

			wealth = -300
			piety = 300
		}

		revoke_allowed = {
			always = no
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					piety = 1000
					NOT = { wealth = 1000 }
					AND = {
						NOT = { controls_religion = sol_boreas_reformed }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.002 # Slow it down
			}
		}
	}
